[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTYPE_Lab_DBL, Intent, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m872[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m873[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m874[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m875[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mcmsSignalError[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm ->ContextID, cmsERROR_COLORSPACE_CHECK, [0m[32m"Cannot create[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mtransform Profile -> Lab"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m876[0m[39m:        return FALSE;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m877[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m878[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m879[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m channels are allowed[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m880[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash occurs because `EmitCIEBasedDEF` immediately dereferences [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Pipeline->Elements` via calls to `[0m[1;35mcmsStageInputChannels[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and subsequently [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without ensuring that `Pipeline` or `Pipeline->Elements` is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-NULL.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `WriteInputLUT` duplicates an empty pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone with no stages[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpasses that empty pipeline to `EmitCIEBasedDEF`, leading to the null-pointer read [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `cmsStageType`.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: src/cmsps2.c[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Function: `EmitCIEBasedDEF`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Approximate lines: [0m[1;36m754[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m763[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. At the very beginning of `EmitCIEBasedDEF`, add a guard clause to verify that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboth `Pipeline` and `Pipeline->Elements` are non-NULL. If this precondition fails, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately return `FALSE` to signal failure and prevent any further dereferences.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Optionally, log an error via `cmsSignalError` if desired, but it is [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msufficient to return `FALSE` so that the calling code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`WriteInputLUT` → [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`GenerateCSA` → `cmsGetPostScriptCSA`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will cleanly exit through its existing error[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths without crashing.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. No other modifications are necessary because downstream functions already [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck the Boolean return value and abort CSA generation safely on failure.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Example Patch Sketch[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m In src/cmsps2.c[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   int [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsIOHANDLER* m, cmsPipeline* Pipeline,[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       cmsUInt32Number Intent, cmsCIEXYZ* BlackPoint[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Guard against null or empty pipeline to avoid null-pointer deref[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline == NULL || Pipeline->Elements == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Optional: [0m[1;35mcmsSignalError[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm->ContextID, cmsERROR_INTERNAL, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m             [0m[32m"Empty pipeline passed to EmitCIEBasedDEF"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return FALSE;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       const char* PreMaj;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       const char* PostMaj;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       const char* PreMin, *PostMin;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       cmsStage* mpe;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       mpe = Pipeline->Elements;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       switch [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageInputChannels[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing logic[0m[33m...[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Change**: Only one function is patched, preserving the existing code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflow and core logic.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Safety**: The guard prevents dereferencing a NULL stage pointer, eliminating[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe segfault reported by AddressSanitizer.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Error Propagation**: Returning `FALSE` triggers the existing error paths in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`WriteInputLUT` and `GenerateCSA`, causing CSA generation to abort gracefully [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than crash.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Test Integrity**: No harness or test code is modified. Existing test [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcoverage and fuzzing behavior remain unchanged; invalid pipelines now fail safely [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of segfaulting.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No External Impact**: The patch does not touch external libraries, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutilities, or harness code—only the vulnerable routine in the source.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Side Effect**: CSA generation will now return no output [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencountering an empty pipeline rather than producing an [0m[1;39m([0m[39minvalid[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m PostScript [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdictionary.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Empty pipelines are not semantically valid in the PostScript [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCSA context. If any legitimate code path intentionally passes an empty pipeline, it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be reviewed and corrected; otherwise, the early return is appropriate.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Monitoring**: After patching, run the full regression and fuzz suite to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure no new failures or behavioral changes in valid pipeline scenarios.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Next Steps[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apply the patch to `EmitCIEBasedDEF` as described.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the OSS-Fuzz target `cms_postscript_fuzzer` to confirm the null-deref [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis resolved.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run full test suite to verify no regressions.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m754[0m[39m:int [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsIOHANDLER* m, cmsPipeline* Pipeline, cmsUInt32Number [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIntent, cmsCIEXYZ* BlackPoint[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m755[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m756[0m[39m:    const char* PreMaj;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m757[0m[39m:    const char* PostMaj;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m758[0m[39m:    const char* PreMin, *PostMin;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m759[0m[39m:    cmsStage* mpe;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m760[0m[39m:        [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m761[0m[39m:    mpe = Pipeline->Elements;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m762[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m763[0m[39m:    switch [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageInputChannels[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/cmsps2.[0m[1;92mc:897[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m907[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m897[0m[39m:            DeviceLink = [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineDup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mv ->Lut[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m898[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDeviceLink == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m899[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mcmsDeleteTransform[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m900[0m[39m:                return FALSE;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m901[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m902[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m903[0m[39m:            dwFlags |= cmsFLAGS_FORCE_CLUT;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m904[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35m_cmsOptimizePipeline[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm->ContextID, &DeviceLink, Intent, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&InputFormat, &OutFrm, &dwFlags[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m905[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m906[0m[39m:            rc = [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, DeviceLink, Intent, [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&BlackPointAdaptedToD50[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m907[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDeviceLink[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;            [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/cmslut.[0m[1;92mc:741[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m750[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m741[0m[39m:    return [0m[1;35m_cmsQuickSaturateWord[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m742[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m743[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m744[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m745[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This routine does a sweep on whole input space, and calls its callback[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m746[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m function on knots. returns TRUE if all ok, FALSE otherwise.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m747:c[0m[39mmsBool CMSEXPORT [0m[1;35mcmsStageSampleCLut16bit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsStage* mpe, cmsSAMPLER16 Sampler, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvoid * Cargo, cmsUInt32Number dwFlags[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m748[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m749[0m[39m:    int i, t, index, rest;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m750[0m[39m:    cmsUInt32Number nTotalPoints;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash in `cmsStageType` indicates that a malformed or incomplete [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`cmsStage` pointer is being passed in. The existing guard in `EmitCIEBasedDEF` only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks that `Pipeline` and `Pipeline->Elements` are non-NULL, but does not verify [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe integrity or expected layout of the stage list. As a result, `mpe = [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPipeline->Elements;` may be non-NULL yet point to a stage whose `.Next` pointer is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL or whose internal `Data` union is invalid, leading `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdereference garbage and SEGV.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing PostScript color resource generation steps [0m[1;39m([0m[39mduplication, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moptimization, black-point adaptation, LUT emission[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must continue to execute for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid pipelines.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter the harness or fuzzing logic; our changes only live inside [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/cmsps2.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand, if needed, minor additional checks in `src/cmslut.c` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Outline[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Strengthen `EmitCIEBasedDEF`[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - At the very start of the function, after confirming `Pipeline != NULL`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraverse and validate the first two stages:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Ensure `Pipeline->Elements` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcall it `mpe0`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is non-NULL.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Ensure `mpe0->Next` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcall it `mpe1`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is non-NULL.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Optionally, loop through the list to count stages and require a minimum [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., ≥ [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m for curve+CLUT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Verify that `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` match the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected first two stage types [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor instance, curve then CLUT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • If any check fails, return `FALSE` immediately to abort PostScript [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39memission for invalid pipelines.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This robust pre-check prevents any call to `cmsStageInputChannels`, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`cmsStageType`, or other stage-based operations on malformed or truncated stage [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlists.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Mirror Validation in `WriteInputLUT`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before calling `EmitCIEBasedDEF` on the optimized `DeviceLink` pipeline, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperform the same integrity checks:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • `DeviceLink != NULL` and `DeviceLink->Elements != NULL`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • The first two stages are present and of the correct types.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • If invalid, free `DeviceLink` and return `FALSE` without invoking [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`EmitCIEBasedDEF`.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This early guard catches malformed pipelines right after [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduplication/optimization, avoiding the deeper call into `cmsStageType`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Defensive Pattern from `cmsStageSampleCLut16bit`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Review `cmsStageSampleCLut16bit` in `cmslut.c` which returns `FALSE` on any[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull or out-of-bounds access. If there are other internal stage-walker utilities [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused by `EmitCIEBasedDEF`, apply similar null checks before dereferencing the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Data` union of a stage.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Step-by-Step Implementation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `src/cmsps2.c`, at the top of `EmitCIEBasedDEF`:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        a. Check `Pipeline != NULL`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        b. Let `cmsStage* mpe0 = Pipeline->Elements;`  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           – If `mpe0 == NULL`, return `FALSE`.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        c. Let `cmsStage* mpe1 = mpe0->Next;`  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           – If `mpe1 == NULL`, return `FALSE`.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        d. If needed, traverse `mpe1->Next` to count stages or detect unexpected [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextra stages.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        e. Use `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to confirm they match [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe expected element types [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurve then CLUT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. If mismatch, return `FALSE`.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In `src/cmsps2.c`, in `WriteInputLUT` before line calling `EmitCIEBasedDEF`:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        a. After `DeviceLink = [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineDup[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` succeeds, and after [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moptimization, repeat the same [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-stage validation.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        b. If validation fails, call `[0m[1;35mcmsPipelineFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDeviceLink[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `return [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFALSE;` to keep resource management correct.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptionally[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `src/cmslut.c`, inspect `cmsStageType` and ensure it only [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minspects the stage’s `Type` field, not internal `Data` pointers. If it already [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdereferences `Data`, wrap those paths with null-checks.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By validating the pipeline structure early and explicitly, we prevent any [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream call from receiving a malformed `cmsStage` pointer.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach preserves all existing logic for valid pipelines and only bails [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout when pipelines are incomplete or of unsupported layout, matching the defensive [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstyle seen in `cmsStageSampleCLut16bit`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or fuzzer-related code is modified; tests for valid PostScript [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput remain unchanged. Invalid or unexpected pipelines simply yield `FALSE`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is already how other failure modes propagate in this module.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side-Effect Mitigation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returning `FALSE` from `EmitCIEBasedDEF` causes the caller to abort PostScript[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCSA emission. Upstream callers check this return value and handle cleanup [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriately [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., freeing transforms[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If downstream code expects a more specific error code, we can document that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FALSE` now covers [0m[32m"unsupported pipeline shape"[0m[39m in the module’s changelog.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broad exception swallowing is introduced; only explicit structure [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation is added.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Reference Pattern[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This strategy mirrors the guard clauses in `cmsStageSampleCLut16bit`, which [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrate correct handling of nil pointers and invalid dimensional data before [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many heavy processing.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar early validation exists in color management routines that only accept [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecific pipeline shapes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., curve-only or matrix-only pipelines[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so our change[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis consistent with library conventions.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                   [0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.END                      ]8;id=525113;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=992777;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mn evals: [1;36m3[0m, patch status: PatchStatus.SOUND[1m)[0m                                        [2m               [0m
